Futureman: private static string ReplaceArgs(string message, Dictionary<string, object> args)         {             if (args == null || args.Count < 1)             {                 return message;             }              foreach (var pair in args)             {                 var s0 = "{" + pair.Key + "}";                 var s1 = pair.Key;                 var s2 = pair.Value != null ? pair.Value.ToString() : "null";                 message = message.Replace(s0, s2);                 message = message.Replace(s1, s2);             }              return message;         }
